`A²*c0 + A*c1*log(A*c2+1) + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*sin(A^c7*c8 + c9)`

The sin argument is `A^c7*c8 + c9`, not `log(A+1)`. Cannot match cos(log(A+1)). **NO MATCH**

For all remaining candidates without sin(log) or cos(log) structure, they cannot match. Let me quickly verify candidates 1-50, 52-66, 69, 71-76, 78-85, 87-88, 90, 92-105:

None of these contain `sin(c*log(...)+c)` or `cos(log(...))`, so they cannot produce the required basis function.
